           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwikitest.alfresco.com%2Fwiki%2F%23caching" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">cache control</a> section of the web script definition.
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            mustRevalidate: (read/write boolean) control whether cache 
           <strong>must</strong> re-validate its version of the web script response to ensure freshness. If not set, the default value is specified by the 
           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwikitest.alfresco.com%2Fwiki%2F%23caching" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">cache control</a> section of the web script definition.
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            maxAge: (read/write long) specifies the maximum amount of time (in seconds, relative to the time of request) that the response will be considered fresh. If not set, the default value is null.
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            lastModified: (read/write date) specifies the time that the content of the response last changed. If not set, the default value is null.
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            ETag: (read/write string) specifies a unique identifier that changes each time the content of the response changes. If not set, the default value is null.
           <br>
          </dt>
         </dl>
         <br>
         <h2>format</h2>
         <br>
         <p>The format of the response.<br></p>
         <br>
         <dl>
          <dt>
            name: (read only) 
           <a class="jive-link-external-small" href="https://community.alfresco.com/external-link.jspa?url=http%3A%2F%2Fwikitest.alfresco.com%2Fwiki%2F3.0_Web_Scripts_Framework%23HTTP_Response_Formats" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">format</a> name
           <br>
          </dt>
         </dl>
         <br>
         <dl>
          <dt>
            mimetype: (read only) mimetype associated with format
           <br>
          </dt>
         </dl>
         <br>
         <h2>json</h2>
         <br>
         <p>If the content is JSON then an object called 'json' is added to the model.<br></p>
         <p>The json object is either a JSONArray or JSONObject depending upon whether the content is an array or not.<br></p>
         <br>
         <h3>jsonUtils</h3>
         <br>
         <p>jsonUtils allows access to the json data from the controller script.<br></p>
         <br>
         <ul>
          <li>var jsonData = jsonUtils.toObject(requestbody.content);<br></li>
          <li>var jsonString = jsonUtils.toJSONString(object);<br></li>
         </ul>
         <h3>JSONArray</h3>
         <br>
         <p>These are the commonly used methods of JSONArray.<br></p>
         <br>
         <ul>
          <li>length()<br></li>
          <li>getJSONObject(index)<br></li>
         </ul>
         <p><br><br></p>
         <br>
         <h3>JSONObject</h3>
         <br>
         <p>These are the commonly used methods of JSONObject.<br></p>
         <br>
         <ul>
          <li>get(fieldName)<br></li>
          <li>has(filedName)<br></li>
          <li>isNull(fieldName)<br></li>
          <li>getJSONArray(fieldName)<br></li>
         </ul>
         <h2>atom</h2>
         <br>
         <p>TODO:<br></p>
         <br>
         <h2>server</h2>
         <br>
         <p>An associative array of meta-data properties that describe the hosting Alfresco server.<br></p>
         <br>
         <dl>
          <dt>
            versionMajor: server major version number, for example 
           <strong>1</strong>.2.3
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            versionMinor: server minor version number, for example 1.
           <strong>2</strong>.3
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            versionRevision: server revision number, for example 1.2.
           <strong>3</strong>
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            versionLabel: server version label, for example Dev
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            versionBuild: server build number, for example build-1
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            version: server version, for example major.minor.revision (label)
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            edition: server edition, for example Enterprise
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            schema: server schema, for example 10
           <br>
          </dt>
         </dl>
         <br>
         <h2>webscript</h2>
         <br>
         <p>An associative array of meta-data properties describing the web script.<br></p>
         <br>
         <dl>
          <dt>
            id: The web script Id
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            shortName: The web script short name
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            description: The web script description
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            defaultFormat: The default response format if none explicitly specified in web script URL
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            formatStyle: The accepted ways of specifying the format in the web script URL
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            URIs: A (string) array of URL templates
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            method: HTTP Method
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            requiredAuthentication: required level of authentication
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            requiredTransaction: required level of transaction
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            storePath: the path of the persistent store where the web script is stored
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            scriptPath: the path (within storePath) of web script implementation files
           <br>
          </dt>
          <dt>
            descPath: the path (within storePath) of the web script description document
           <br>
          </dt>
         </dl>
        </div>
